# -*- ck2.events -*-
# Audax Validator EnableCommentMetadata

# Written by zijistark via trait-notify.pl v1.03 on Wed Aug  3 06:47:48 2016 (Pacific)

#########################################
#       TRAIT NOTIFICATION EVENTS       #
#########################################

namespace = emf_notify

# NOTE: One should never call these event IDs directly but instead should use
# the named scripted effects in emf_notify_effects.txt to deliver notifications
# for the add/remove of traits. That way, when traits are added or changed,
# their trait IDs and thus event IDs here may change, but their named effects
# will always resolve to the correct event. Additionally, the scripted effects
# actually add/remove the trait as well so as to be able to avoid redundant
# notifications and catch coding errors.


##################################################
#    Trait Gain Notification Forwarder Events    #
# emf_notify.1 through emf_notify.1000 reserved  #
##################################################

# emf_notify.1 -- added amateurish_plotter (Amateurish Plotter)
# Audax Validator "." Ignore_1005
character_event = {
	id = emf_notify.1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:emf_notify_char = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.2001 } }
	}
}

# emf_notify.2001 -- added amateurish_plotter (Amateurish Plotter) to FROM [notification]
# Audax Validator "." Ignore_1005
character_event = {
	id = emf_notify.2001
	picture = GFX_evt_emissary

	desc = {
		text = emf_notify.2001.desc_self
		trigger = { character = FROM }
	}
	desc = {
		text = emf_notify.2001.desc_councillor
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_councillor = yes
				vassal_of = ROOT
			}
			NOR = {
				character = FROM
				is_close_relative = FROM
				any_spouse = { character = FROM }
				any_ward = { character = FROM }
				guardian = { character = FROM }
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = emf_notify.2001.desc_relation
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_close_relative = FROM
				any_spouse = { character = FROM }
				any_ward = { character = FROM }
				guardian = { character = FROM }
			}
			NOR = {
				character = FROM
				FROM = {
					is_councillor = yes
					vassal_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = emf_notify.2001.desc
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = FROM
				FROM = {
					is_councillor = yes
					vassal_of = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					is_close_relative = FROM
					any_spouse = { character = FROM }
					any_ward = { character = FROM }
					guardian = { character = FROM }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	notification = yes

	option = { name = OK }
}

				is_close_relative = FROM

				any_ward = { character = FROM }

			NOR = {
				character = FROM

					is_councillor = yes
					vassal_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = emf_notify.2054.desc
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = FROM
				FROM = {
					is_councillor = yes
					vassal_of = ROOT

				character = FROM
				FROM = {
					is_councillor = yes
					vassal_of = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					is_close_relative = FROM
					any_spouse = { character = FROM }
					any_ward = { character = FROM }
					guardian = { character = FROM }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	notification = yes

	option = { name = OK }
}

		text = emf_notify.3222.desc_self
		trigger = { character = FROM }
	}
	desc = {

		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_councillor = yes
				vassal_of = ROOT
			}
			NOR = {
				character = FROM
				is_close_relative = FROM
				any_spouse = { character = FROM }
				any_ward = { character = FROM }
				guardian = { character = FROM }
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = emf_notify.3222.desc_relation
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_close_relative = FROM
				any_spouse = { character = FROM }
				any_ward = { character = FROM }
				guardian = { character = FROM }
			}
			NOR = {
				character = FROM
				FROM = {
					is_councillor = yes
					vassal_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
